Tense Political Situation in Japan 61

Regarding the Seiyukai's Bomb Motion

The Government Does Not Hesitate to Fight to the End

(Tokyo) Regarding the aftermath of the bomb motion, the government has stated its policy of adding a second reserve fund. However, the government has adopted a tough stance and abandoned the compromise with the Seiyukai because the Seiyukai has persistently pursued the disciplinary issues of Tokuji Tokonami and others, which has harmed the intentions of the government's leading figures such as Takahashi Korekiyo, Minister of Finance. They have therefore accepted the tough opinions of the Minseito. If the Seiyukai acknowledges the establishment of the reserve fund, there will be no problems for the party. If they disagree, the government has stated that it will not hesitate to face a head-on collision. Therefore, the attitude of the Seiyukai is noteworthy. However, the government's observation is that even if the Seiyukai stops questioning the bomb motion due to the establishment of the reserve fund, they will attack issues such as the temporary excess profits tax and disciplinary problems. Therefore, since a tough stance has been adopted on the bomb motion, the attitude on other issues should not be changed either. If the Seiyukai launches an attack, they will not hesitate to fight to the end. Since the government has this awareness, the tense state of the political situation is difficult to resolve. (Dentsu dispatch of the 9th)

(Tokyo) After the budget general meeting adjourned, the Seiyukai held a general affairs meeting. The government ignored the Seiyukai's demands and only attempted to muddle through by spending the second reserve fund. The hardliners within the party were very indignant, but the self-respecting faction also did not want to adopt a mediating attitude because their suggestions were not accepted by the government. The overall policy of the Seiyukai is to pass the government's budget bill first, and then challenge the government with issues such as disciplinary problems, the temporary excess profits tax, and the local finance allocation law. Therefore, conflict between the government and the Seiyukai is inevitable in the future. (Japan United Press dispatch of the 9th)

(Tokyo) The Minseito believes that the cabinet decision made last night reflects the party's demands, especially the point of explicitly convening an extraordinary session of the Diet. They consider it satisfactory, decided to support the government, and are watching the Seiyukai's measures with a tough attitude. (Dentsu dispatch of the 9th)

U.S. Silver Purchases Significantly Reduced in the Past Week 62

(Washington) According to today's weekly report from the Department of Commerce, the total value of silver imported into the United States in the week ending February 1 was $3,498,000. The previous week was $8,406,000, and the week before that was $5,498,000. By comparison, it can be seen that the amount of silver imported into the United States in the past week has been greatly reduced, and the active progress of the U.S. Treasury Department's silver purchase program can also be seen. Although the amount of silver entering the United States in the week after January 18 reached as much as $8,406,000, part of it was purchased by the Treasury Department in the past and is not being actively purchased by the U.S. government now. Today, 12 million ounces of silver were shipped from London, some of which will be delivered to the New York Federal Reserve Bank. This batch of silver was purchased in succession using the exchange stabilization fund when the U.S. dollar was strong. (Reuters dispatch of the 8th)

Black Spot Discovered on the Sun 63

Diameter Greater Than Six Times That of the Earth

Great Impact on Atmospheric Currents

(Berlin) Astronomers here discovered a huge black spot on the western side of the solar disk yesterday. Its diameter is estimated to be 70,000 kilometers, more than six times the diameter of the Earth. The sunspot seen in recent years is the largest this time. (Havas dispatch of the 8th)

(Berlin) In the bright and cloudless spring days, a large black spot was suddenly discovered on the sun, located in the western part of the solar disk and very clear. According to measurements by German astronomers, the diameter of the black spot is between 60,000 and 70,000 kilometers, while the diameter of the Earth is only 10,000 kilometers. Therefore, an area ten times the size of the Earth would be needed to cover this black spot. According to observations from Earth, it is often possible to discover black spots, but according to speculation, it occurs once every eleven years, so there are few such large spots. However, this black spot may even exist for another twelve or thirteen days. Studies have shown that black spots in the sun have a great impact on atmospheric currents, because they can disrupt the current balance between the planets and can also hinder magnetic needles and affect navigation, aviation, and telephone and wireless communication. (Guomin dispatch of the 8th)

Strengthening the coastal defenses of the Hawaiian Islands and the Alaskan Peninsula, requiring an expenditure of $2,000,000; 4. Mechanizing the army, requiring an expenditure of $16,000,000; 5. Modernizing infantry and artillery weapons, requiring an expenditure of $8,000,000. Military leaders and members of the Senate Army Committee held a secret meeting today to discuss this plan. This is the first such meeting since Japan announced the abrogation of the Washington Naval Treaty last December. According to Senator McNally, a member of the committee, the decisions made at this meeting are purely defensive in nature, and even if Japan had not announced the abrogation of the Washington Naval Treaty, the United States would have made this decision. Simon Delivers Speech on Peace at Banquet of Paris Chamber of Commerce 75

The work we have completed in London is not intended to oppose anyone. We have no intention of establishing a narrow agreement. What we seek is to establish a plan that can serve as a basis for free and equal discussions between all parties concerned, so that the foundation of peace can be more stable. I believe that there will be great progress in 1935. In the political field, international mutual trust will increase day by day. In terms of trade, prosperity can also be gradually restored." Foreign Secretary Simon arrived here from London with his wife this afternoon and will return to Britain tomorrow afternoon. The Foreign Secretary's visit is purely of a private nature. Foreign Minister Laval is suffering from influenza and is resting at home, so he could not attend the banquet to meet with Simon. (Havas dispatch of the 8th)

London Anglo-French Agreement Seeks to Gauge German Intentions 77

Italy Expresses Conditional Participation in Air Pact

Mutual Obligations Between Britain and Italy Must Be Excluded

(Moscow) The French "Moscow Daily News" published an editorial summarizing the views of relevant authorities, stating, "The agreement reached in London by British Foreign Secretary Simon and French Foreign Minister Laval will allow the world to understand Germany's true intentions. This agreement is not without ambiguity. For example, while there is no explicit indication whether Britain is willing to restrain Germany's ambitions in Eastern Europe, the Soviet government should still consider the principles stipulated in this agreement helpful to its own interests. Furthermore, after the conclusion of the London agreement, Moscow raised some reservations about France's actions in consolidating peace in Eastern Europe. However, after the French Ambassador to Russia, Alphand, delivered the original text of the London Declaration and provided oral explanations, the content of the agreement was fully understood. The London agreement invites Germany to participate in the Western European Air Pact and offers extremely important rewards (referring to the abolition of the Versailles Treaty's armament clauses). At the same time, it forces Germany to cease making excuses to refuse international cooperation. Even the bilateral treaties that Germany currently advocates must be abandoned, and the advantages of regional mutual assistance pacts must be recognized. If Germany accepts participation in the Western European Air Pact but still refuses to cooperate in Eastern Europe, it would be tantamount to tacitly admitting Germany's ambition to annex Soviet territory. Conversely, if Germany refuses to cooperate entirely, even refusing to participate in the Western European Pact, then Germany is provoking world opinion and all friends of world peace, and Britain and France would be unable to forgive Germany. In short, the London agreement clearly indicates to Germany that Britain and France want a swift response and are unwilling to engage in endless haggling with Germany. Moreover, French Foreign Minister Laval and Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov signed the Franco-Russian Agreement in Geneva on December 5th of last year (agreeing not to conclude agreements with other countries during the negotiation period of the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact that could hinder these negotiations), which is more than sufficient to deal with everything," and so on. (Havas, 9th)

(Rome) A communiqué was issued here today, formally stating that Italy is willing to participate in the Anglo-Franco-German-Belgian negotiated Air Pact under certain conditions. The communiqué stated that Italy's position regarding the pact will be decided soon based on a compromise approach in principle, and attention will be paid to the relative special circumstances between Britain and Italy. It is noted that the conclusion of the pact was proposed by Britain and France recently in London, with the sole purpose of consolidating peace. The signatory states undertake to provide air force assistance if any signatory is subjected to an unprovoked air attack by another country. (Reuters, 9th)

(London) Regarding Italy's attitude towards the London Anglo-French Agreement, after the Italian government issued a communiqué, political figures believe that the revisions Italy hopes for should be discussed by all countries assuming the signing of the Air Pact before a decision can be made. It is generally believed that the reservations put forward by Italy are the same as the news released by Britain yesterday, that is, Italy accepts the joint signing of the Air Pact by the signatory countries of the Locarno Treaty, but with a separate protocol stipulating that all of Italy's obligations to Britain should be excluded. (Havas, 9th)

(London) Italy cannot participate in the Air Pact proposed by Britain and France. According to well-informed sources in Britain, Italy's attitude is based on factual reasons. The pact plan stipulates that if one of the signatory countries is attacked by another country's air force, it should jointly resist it. Its nature is entirely mutual. However, as far as Britain and Italy are concerned, Italy believes that sending an air force to Britain to assist in the war is practically impossible, just as it is imaginable that the British air force cannot assist in defending Italian territory. However, Italy agrees that an Air Pact should be signed between the signatory countries of the Locarno Pact, including Italy, but with a separate protocol stipulating that Italy does not bear any obligations to Britain (referring to air force assistance to Britain). As for the issue of mutual air force assistance between Italy and France, the Italian diplomatic authorities have not raised any reservations. (Havas, 8th)

Italian Newspapers' Anti-German Sentiment 78

German Newspapers Write Articles Criticizing

(Berlin) The Essen City National Daily, the organ of Prussian Governor Goering, wrote an article today attacking the Italian newspapers' views on the Anglo-French declaration, stating, "The Italian newspapers' views clearly show anti-German sentiment, especially the recent articles in the People's Daily. At a time when European countries are preparing to form a broad front to stabilize the situation, it is surprising that Italian newspapers have such views. Germany has not yet responded to the proposals of Britain and France. All relevant countries should remain calm and not hastily conclude that the only danger lies on the German side." (Havas, 8th)

Germany Advocates National Self-Determination for Austria 79

Condition for Joining the Central European Pact

(Vienna) According to news from Berlin, regarding Germany's participation in the Central European Non-Interference Pact, the German government's reply is expected to put forward a condition advocating that Austria should have the right to national self-determination. In other words, to hold a plebiscite to decide Austria's fate. Austrian sources believe this news is not credible. If Germany makes such a demand, it would be interfering in Austria's internal affairs. If Germany allows itself to participate in the Non-Interference Pact, it should not be so contradictory. Moreover, Austria, based on the vocational association system, established a Christian Germanic nation-state, which was originally based on the people's self-determination. Austria used its own army to eliminate the rebellions of the National Socialist Party and Marxism, without relying on outsiders. As for other countries forcing Austria to hold a plebiscite, or advising Austria to hold a plebiscite, it is all unacceptable to Austria. Regarding this, Chancellor Schuschnigg declared, "The Austrian plebiscite must wait until the Austrian government believes the time has come and it is done voluntarily by Austria, and it must never follow the will of foreign governments." In short, if Germany responds to the proposals of Britain and France in this way, the result will be greatly regrettable. (Havas, 8th)

Diamonds Can Be Distinguished Under a Microscope 91

Bubbles in the Center Indicate Little Value

(London) A former jeweler, claiming to have worked as a secret tester in London for 45 years, has created a diamond indistinguishable from a real one. A real one is worth hundreds of pounds, while his artificial one costs only fifteen pounds. The jewelry industry was greatly alarmed. The London Chamber of Commerce's Diamond and Jewelry Industry Department sent experts to investigate. A formal report was released last night stating that after inspection, the so-called artificial diamond does not contain any diamond substance. Its refractive index and specific gravity are very different from those of a real one. When observed under a microscope, small gas bubbles appear in the center. This kind of imitation diamond has very little commercial value and cannot be used for industrial purposes. All diamond merchants and experts can distinguish its authenticity. According to previous reports, a curio dealer named Gerard in the West End of London claimed that an old man over seventy years old had invented a method of artificially manufacturing diamonds and would bring a diamond, which he estimated to be worth about 400 pounds. The old man later said that it was an artificial stone, and he was greatly mistaken. He had purchased the exclusive rights to sell this artificial diamond. Gerard will be disappointed now that he has seen the expert's report. (Reuters, 8th)

America's Poverty Relief Policies (New York Correspondence) 116

Urban Industrial Decline, Rural Scene Slightly Better. The implementation of the NRA in the United States has had minimal effect, necessitating a shift to a "new policy." Last summer, the general economic situation improved significantly, but with the arrival of winter, due to seasonal factors, it declined again. In November 1934, the manufacturing and mining industries employed 86,000 fewer workers than in October, which means the number of unemployed increased. Simultaneously, the wages paid by these industries decreased by US$3,915,000, reducing workers' income. If seasonal factors are disregarded, the decline is not considered severe. In November, worker employment only decreased by 1.9% compared to October, while wages decreased by 2.5%. This proves that the American economy is still struggling, and genuine recovery seems quite distant.

Therefore, at the end of November 1934, Federal Emergency Relief Administrator Harry Hopkins advised President Roosevelt, advocating for "completely eradicating poverty in America." The outlines of the EPIA (End Poverty in America) proposal include the following:

(1) Social insurance plan.

(2) Expanding programs to assist farmers and rescue rural areas.

(3) Mass transfer of those living on land with livelihood difficulties to cultured residential areas.

(4) Providing farmers with loans from the national treasury to purchase farm tools and livestock.

(5) Expanding programs for unemployed workers to work in factories.

(6) Planning to allocate large-scale, inexpensive housing to those who cannot become agricultural migrants.

Except for the allocation of inexpensive housing, the remaining items, though small in scale, have been implemented, but their help to the actual economic phenomena in the United States is not significant. Therefore, "Hopkins" believes that if relief costs are to be saved, factories operated by the federal government can come forward to accommodate the unemployed, requiring them to produce according to their own needs, implementing the exchange of products, crops, and goods, but not paying wages. This may save some relief costs, but it is uncertain.

Since the implementation of the NRA policy until now, the Roosevelt government has indeed made its utmost efforts. Though not necessarily effective, it has managed to maintain the status quo. As for the above-mentioned EPIA plan, the total cost required is estimated to be US$90 billion. Assuming its implementation period is two years, it would require an annual expenditure of US$45 billion. Whether satisfactory results can be obtained after implementation remains questionable. However, there is no doubt that today's America needs a large-scale poverty relief movement. Therefore, implementing inflationary policies is also a necessity. If not, the future and current dangers may become even more extensive.

Fortunately, there was a slight increase in some sectors at the beginning of winter. For example, the number of workers in the agricultural tool industry increased by 9.1% in November compared to the previous month. The number of workers in department stores and mail-order businesses also increased by 6.4%. The coal industry, due to increased winter demand, saw a 3.8% increase in coal miners. This certainly has some seasonal factors, but it also contains some elements of economic improvement.

Economic panic is particularly severe in rural areas, especially after the autumn of 1932. Agricultural products fell by 35% compared to before the war, while the prices of industrial manufactured goods they needed rose by 7%. Therefore, the purchasing power of farmers was only 61% of that before the war. This reflected back to the cities, naturally deepening the degree of panic. However, since last autumn, the situation in rural areas has gradually improved. Farmers' income increased from US$5.48 billion in 1933 to US$6.5 billion (which included US$610 million in agricultural relief funds). Compared to the previous year, it still increased by 22%, and rural purchasing power (at the end of November) had risen to 82% of that before the war. Therefore, the agricultural tool industry and others have improved. Unfortunately, this is still a local phenomenon. The 11 million unemployed have not changed much. (January 12th)

Legislative Yuan Passes Transaction Tax Regulations 117

The Legislative Yuan held its fourth meeting on the 8th to discuss the draft of the Stock Exchange Transaction Tax Regulations and resolved to approve the amended version. The text of the regulations and the review report are recorded below:

Stock Exchange Transaction Tax Regulations Article 1: All transactions of securities or goods on the stock exchange shall be subject to transaction tax in accordance with the provisions of these regulations. Article 2: The tax rates for the transaction tax are as follows: A. For securities, the tax shall be levied on the agreed price of the transaction. The amount below one hundred yuan in the price shall be calculated as one hundred yuan. No tax shall be levied on spot transactions. For transactions with a delivery period within seven days, the tax shall be 0.04% of the price. For transactions with a delivery period beyond seven days, the tax shall be 0.07% of the price. B. For gold bars (312.50 grams, fineness 978), the tax shall be 7 li of national currency per bar. C. For cotton, the tax shall be 45 cents of national currency per 100 dan. D. For cotton yarn, the tax shall be 1 yuan and 75 cents of national currency per 100 bales. E. For flour, the tax shall be 35 cents of national currency per 1,000 bags. F. For miscellaneous grains, wheat, soybeans, and red sorghum, the tax shall be 35 cents of national currency per vehicle. For soybean cakes, the tax shall be 20 cents of national currency per 1,000 pieces. For soybean oil, the tax shall be 20 cents of national currency per 100 dan. Article 3: The transaction tax shall be collected by the stock exchange from the parties involved in the transaction at the time of the transaction, according to the tax rates stipulated in Article 2, with each party bearing half of the tax. The exchange is responsible for collecting it from the original broker and remitting it together. If the broker fails to collect or delivers an insufficient amount, the stock exchange shall be responsible for paying it on behalf of the broker. Article 4: The stock exchange shall fill out a clear table of the daily transaction volume and prices on the following day, report it to the stock exchange supervisor for verification, and directly pay the transaction tax to the national treasury. Article 5: The stock exchange supervisor may inspect the stock exchange's or broker's books at any time to verify whether there is any concealment or falsification of the transaction volume and prices reported by the stock exchange. Article 6: If the stock exchange fails to make the report in Article 4, pay taxes, violates the prescribed time limit, or the report contains concealment or falsification, it shall be fined up to 500 yuan. If tax evasion results, in addition to collecting the tax payable, a fine of 10 to 30 times the amount of tax evaded shall be imposed. If the stock exchange is penalized due to a broker's violation of regulations, it may transfer the responsibility to the broker. Article 7: If the types of goods traded on the stock exchange are increased or changed, the tax rate shall be revised according to legislative procedures, and the transaction tax shall be levied. Article 8: For transaction taxes in places where transaction tax supervisors are stationed, the Ministry of Finance may entrust local financial authorities or banks to collect and remit them on its behalf. Article 9: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Review Report: To jointly report. The draft Transaction Tax Regulations case was resolved at the 85th meeting of the previous session of the Yuan and referred to the Finance Committee and the Economic Committee for review, etc. In accordance with this, the first joint meeting of this committee and others was held on January 24th to discuss the matter. Representatives from the Ministry of Finance, the Federation of Stock Exchanges, and the Brokers Association were invited to attend and provide explanations in advance. After discussion, it was decided to submit it to committee members Chen Changheng, Chen Jianru, Zheng Hongnian, Liu Zhendong, and Zhang Zhihan for preliminary review. Subsequently, the preliminary review report from committee members Chen Changheng and others was received, along with a proposed amendment to the draft Transaction Tax Regulations. This was then presented to the second joint meeting of this committee and others for detailed discussion. The reason for amending the transaction tax rate is that securities are subject to a small tax based on price, with spot transactions being tax-exempt and short-term and long-term futures within the futures period being subject to different rates. In addition, the four types of goods—gold bars, cotton, cotton yarn, and flour—are taxed at one-twentieth of the handling fees in the original "Schedule of Handling Fees for Various Traded Goods." The various items under miscellaneous grains—wheat, soybeans, red sorghum, soybean cakes, and soybean oil—are agricultural, industrial, food, or fertilizer necessities, and the tax should be reduced accordingly. Therefore, it is estimated to be taxed at one-fortieth of the standard in the previous table to show differentiation. We immediately separately passed whether it is appropriate, and we should prepare an amendment and submit it to the Yuan for review and decision. Respectfully presented to the President of the Yuan, Sun, and Vice President Shao, with an attached copy of the proposed amendment to the draft Transaction Tax Regulations. Finance and Economic Committee Chairmen Ma Yinchu and Wu Shangying. (September)

Grand Victory Celebration in Ganzhou 118

Captured Communist Bandit Paraded on Stage for Public Display

Crowds of People Surge to Watch

Nanchang Correspondence: Fang Zhimin, the leader of the Communist bandits in the border area of Jiangxi, Fujian, Zhejiang, and Anhui, was captured alive by the troops of the 43rd Independent Brigade under Liu Zhiqing in the Huaiyu Mountains near Nuanshan on the border of Dexing and Yushan at around 4:00 AM on the 29th of last month. Zhao Guantao escorted him from Shangrao to Nanchang in an armored car on the 2nd of this month. Various circles in the provincial capital specially held a "Jiangxi Circles Celebrating the Capture Alive of Bandit Leader Fang Zhimin and Others Assembly" at the Zhongshan Memorial Hall in Yuzhang Park at 12:00 noon on the 6th. Due to the capacity of the venue, each public organization was only allowed to have ten representatives participate. Various circles flocked to the meeting to catch a glimpse of the bandit leader's face. The military police took extremely thorough precautions and guards, with sentries stationed at every step and posts everywhere. Those without proof of documents from organizations could not enter the meeting. Around 11:00 AM, the Zhongshan Memorial Hall was already packed without any space. Around 12:30 PM, the Military Law Office drove Fang Zhimin directly to Yuzhang Park in an armored car. From Beiyingfang to Yuzhang Road, people lined up on both sides, craning their necks to see Fang Zhimin, forming mountains of people, blocking the road. After the car entered the park, several soldiers escorted Fang Zhimin onto the stage from the east side. The bandit leader, who had poisoned four provinces and wreaked havoc for seven or eight years, causing people to shudder at the thought, suddenly met the crowd at the venue. Fang Zhimin stood on the stage, tall, wearing a gray cloth cotton coat, a blue short coat (both newly changed, as he was tattered and filthy when captured), leggings, blue cloth shoes, a flat-top haircut, and a long face with fair complexion. His eyebrows and eyes were quite clear and handsome, and he was plumper than when he served as the provincial party committee and peasant minister in Nanchang sixteen years ago. His beard was about an inch long and had not been shaved. His unkempt appearance showed his embarrassed state of sleeping in the open air and eating in the wind during his escape. At that time, Fang Zhimin stood hunched on the stage, unable to look up, his spirit was depressed and demoralized, like a tiger entering a cage, his fierce flame completely extinguished. Fang Zhimin was on the stage for about three minutes, and after the political training office took magnesium light photographs, a soldier escorted him off the stage and back to the original place in an armored car. The number of people gathered around Beiyingfang Chen Family Ancestral Hall under the camphor tree increased.

After Fang Zhimin left the stage, the assembly officially began. At this time, the crowd dispersed in a commotion. The police and gendarmerie tried their best to maintain order, and order was restored. Yu Baiqing led the ceremony, reported the meaning of the victory celebration, and mostly encouraged the people to comfort the soldiers. Then Zhao Guantao reported the process of encircling and suppressing Fang Zhimin and capturing him alive. After the report, the adjournment of the meeting was announced.

Sichuan Provincial Chairman Liu Xiang's Inaugural Declaration 119

The members of the Sichuan Provincial Government are scheduled to take office in Chongqing today (the 10th). Chairman Liu Xiang's inaugural declaration is recorded first. Previously, when reporting on his duties in the capital, Chairman Lin, Chairman Chiang, President Wang, and the officials of the central authorities earnestly encouraged him, all believing that with national crisis at hand, stability was especially urgent. The strategy for suppressing bandits emphasized both politics and military affairs. To advance politics, the structure must be transformed first. Therefore, the Yuan decided to reorganize the Sichuan Provincial Government and ordered the provincial chairman to concurrently serve. He firmly declined, but was unsuccessful and reluctantly accepted the burden. Now, as he begins his term, he deeply feels the weight of responsibility. Considering the meaning of "governing without excessive words," he dares not expect too much of himself. However, remembering that he was appointed in a time of crisis, he must act righteously and not yield too much. He respectfully presents his thoughts and what he and his colleagues should encourage each other with to the elders, brothers, and sisters of Sichuan. He respectfully follows the instructions of the Prime Minister, who always said that revolution must first revolutionize the mind. The people of the country observe the situation in Sichuan, often confined to the old saying "Sichuan is the first to be chaotic when the country is not yet in chaos, and Sichuan is not yet governed when the country is already governed," believing that Sichuan is easy to be chaotic and difficult to govern, which has become a historical constant. In fact, the people of Sichuan's courage to uphold righteousness and sincerity to love the country are always at the forefront and have never been willing to lag behind others. For example, the campaigns to overthrow the Manchus, overthrow Yuan, protect the country, and protect the constitution have all made significant contributions to the country. Although this has stirred up internal conflicts and caused years of war, the glorious history is clearly present. What the world calls chaos first and governance later is mostly abandoning the cause to discuss the effect. Moreover, today's Sichuan, its geographical environment and political environment have greatly changed with the internal and external situations. The life of a province is closely related to the entire life of the Republic of China. Saving Sichuan is saving the country, and there is no other responsibility. Since we have this belief, then today's bandit disaster can help to revitalize the country through hardship. As a person from Sichuan, and bearing the full responsibility for governing the province, he should diligently seek governance, make up for mistakes, and strive for merits to protect the reputation of Sichuan. Filling the sea with stones is his unchanging ambition. This is the first thing he wants to encourage all the elders, brothers, and sisters of Sichuan with. In recent years, the people of Sichuan have been frightened by the bandit disaster and eagerly seek governance, believing that suppressing bandits is more important than military affairs and that politics is not urgent. They do not know that today's bandit disaster has a very significant political nature at its root. The doctrines and policies that the communists madly advocate have already exhausted their tricks, as evidenced by the past events in Jiangxi, and are not worth mentioning. However, the reason why the bandits can sell their deceptive tricks is precisely because there are undeniable weaknesses in our politics, giving them an opportunity to take advantage of. If we can consolidate the people's hearts towards goodness, we can block the mouths of the bandits who incite chaos. If our people have a strict organization, then the bandit chiefs become isolated tyrants. Understanding this meaning, we know that corrupt politics can create bandits, and clear politics can suppress bandits. To suppress bandits with politics, the government that produces clear politics must be thoroughly enriched. To enrich the government, a large group of smart and capable people must become a large group, and working together will achieve daily success. From now on, the government's will is the authority of the will of the people of Sichuan. With one heart and one mind, we will fight together. This is the second thing he wants to encourage all the elders, brothers, and sisters of Sichuan with. Since we clearly recognize our mission of the era, the provincial government's measures should focus on the urgent needs of the era and strive to implement them. After September 18th, the enemy maliciously spread propaganda, always denigrating us by saying "China has no organization." The so-called lack of organization means that each province has its own customs, without escaping the remaining poison of feudal separatism. Therefore, China today needs unity, which is the national consensus of the whole country. When we in Sichuan talk about Sichuan, we should take completing a unified provincial government as the only important meaning at present. Where duty lies, we will dedicate ourselves to it, but still base ourselves on the consistent ambition of impartiality and selflessness, taking coexistence and co-prosperity as the goal. The humble foolishness should be understood and forgiven by compatriots. Since the people recognize the need for unity and are so urgently needed, they should immediately catch up and urge progress. This is what Xiang has been thinking about day and night and wants to encourage all the elders, brothers, and sisters of Sichuan with. Last year, Chairman Chiang based on his experience in suppressing bandits with politics and formulated the outline of the provincial government's joint office method. Jiangxi, Hubei, Fujian, and Anhui have successively implemented it, rectifying regulations and disciplines, and the perceptions are refreshed. Sichuan, eager for unity, can use this as a model. The current report clarifies the central government's intention to formulate rules based on the outline and implement them immediately. All important policies of the provincial government will be based on the central government's common laws and regulations. Reading the Prime Minister's speech on the Five-Power Constitution, it is said, "The government is a big machine." He secretly believes that the activities of all machines have rhythm, relying on the two functions of starting and braking. So is the government. Without a strong driving force, politics cannot be promoted. Without a considerable braking force, politics can easily deviate from the right track. The spirit of the outline is to unify the will of the provincial government and increase administrative efficiency, which is to increase the government's power with centralization and prevent the abuse of power with collective decision-making. The obstacles to the government in politics have been eliminated due to the new legal system, so future facilities should be advanced in accordance with the law without any evasion. The suffering of the people's livelihood is now extreme. Saving from drowning and extinguishing fire is urgent. Remembering the past experience, we dare not say that we will succeed in a matter of days, but remembering that the future can be pursued, how can we bear to belittle ourselves, make empty words, and sell reputation? This is what integrity will not do, and pleasing the crowd and seeking tolerance is also what conscience does not allow. Now, after discussing with colleagues again and again, those who sit down and speak and then act together are: First, carefully select virtuous and capable people, refresh official governance, set up a civil servant qualification review committee, publicly select, and prevent seeking advancement by chance, set up regular training classes to cultivate true talents, and the training method focuses on the study of practical problems, and finally determine the best through assessment, without speaking emptily in the chapters, and strive to make all the excellent talents in society find a way to be useful. Once they are employed, they will be assessed in accordance with the law and used to ensure their security. Those who are outstanding in their governance will be promoted especially, and those who are derelict in their duties will be immediately dismissed, and the provincial government will set up a badge committee to discuss and deal with them in accordance with the law. If they are impartial in their promotion and demotion, they will strive to be diligent. Secondly, the departments of civil affairs, finance, construction, and education plan to correct the accumulated habits of standing side by side and boasting about their achievements, and strive to make solid progress within the limits of manpower and financial resources. In civil affairs, we will rectify official integrity, severely punish corruption, be stern and swift, and shift the atmosphere of the official career. In finance, we will reduce expenses and control consumption, cultivate tax sources, and strive to make the economy self-sufficient and reduce imports. In construction, we will improve local products and develop transportation, and strive to benefit the people and achieve cost-effectiveness. In education, we will make learning practical and diligently practice labor, and strive to integrate production and education. In military affairs, we will improve the quality, be refined, strong, and loyal, and strive to eliminate redundancy and gradually tighten. In short, in the year when the people's strength is declining and everything needs to be rebuilt, all of us should make the people trust the government, then they will work without complaint, and make the people's wealth return to the public, then more acquisitions are not abuse. The burden of the people of Sichuan is too heavy, and it has long been exhausting to lift the tripod. Every time I think about it, I feel deeply guilty. Considering that wealth is the mother of all policies, national economy and people's livelihood must be taken care of. The current situation in Sichuan has long been beset by difficulties from top to bottom. If we stick to the old ways, not only will everything be backward, but it will almost be exhausted. It is proposed that the provincial government set up a financial reorganization committee to consult widely and determine a detailed reorganization plan, and immediately cancel all exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous taxes, and separately set unified provincial taxes, so that the people's burden is average, and the collection method should be reasonable, in order to conform to the principles of fairness and universality. In terms of expenditure, it is decided to practice strict economy, work hard, and reduce the expenses of the military and political affairs and issue them to the people, saving one point of material resources for the people, which is to protect one point of vitality for the society. In the midst of encouraging progress, there is still the intention of recuperating and recuperating. Self-examination is not ashamed, and the public will understand. Dare to say that there is no fault, just do your best. All the things mentioned are humble and without high theory. Eating when hungry and drinking when thirsty, the effect is easy to see. My compatriots, friendship is sincere and righteous, and we have shared hardships for a long time. When we are in the same boat through thick and thin, we will be able to help each other. Looking around, we are in a situation where we can only advance and not retreat. It is not too late to mend the fold, and it is a good opportunity given by God. The great disaster in the future is feared to pass quickly. Xiang has experienced the changes of the world and often feels the vicissitudes of life. Serving the hometown and country, he has long been ashamed of his lack of ability. Only this reverence and respect for the homeland have not been forgotten day and night, and he wants to use the inspiration of sincerity to eliminate the great disaster in one or ten thousand. Wuhu Commerce Declines 120

Bank Business Still Okay, Money Lending Mediocre

Rice Business Sluggish, All Industries Find Recovery Difficult

Wuhu Correspondence: Wuhu is the only commercial port in Anhui Province, with convenient transportation, prosperous commerce, and a bustling market. However, the rise and fall of all industries have always depended on the rice market. In recent years, due to the impact of foreign rice dumping, the rice market has been in a slump, and all businesses have been greatly affected. Last year, northern and southern Anhui suffered severe droughts, and southern Anhui counties were plagued by bandits. The market downturn became even more acute, coupled with extremely tight credit. The financial sector did not release large amounts of funds, causing all industries to be in a state of panic. During this difficult period, it was not easy to start a business, and those with insufficient capital were unable to sustain themselves. They laid off shop assistants and tried to tighten their belts. Therefore, after each year's final accounting, countless shop assistants lost their jobs, making life even more difficult, and the social economy became increasingly depressed. According to business practices, after last year's inventory count, the reporter conducted on-site investigations in various industries. Most businesses suffered losses, with only a few managing to cover expenses. In the minds of most businessmen, last year's poor environment had passed away with the old year on New Year's Eve. They only hope that this year's rice market will be active, and that merchants from Guangdong and Chaozhou will boldly engage in business and purchasing, so that Wuhu commerce may have a chance of recovery. The following is a brief overview of the major commercial conditions of last year:

Banks: Wuhu's banking industry has been quite developed in recent years. After the Anhui Bank in Wuhu closed down, the Four Provinces Farmers Bank was added, bringing the total to six banks. Their business is thriving. The Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Shanghai Bank all focus on grain mortgage transactions and provide little to no credit lending. After the year-end closing, there were no bad debt losses, and all banks had profits. According to a recent survey, the banks' mortgage loans are about five million yuan or more, and the total amount of deposits is about ten million yuan. The banks closed for four days during the Spring Festival and added another day for Sunday, resuming business as usual on the 9th.

Money Shops: In the past, money shops were the hub of the financial world. During the active period of the rice market, there were 34 money shops, and their business was extremely prosperous for a time. Each shop had tens of thousands of taels of silver in profit each year. In recent years, rural bankruptcy and market downturns have meant that the industry, which relies on credit lending as its sole business, has suffered huge bad debt losses. Those unable to sustain themselves closed down one after another. Last spring, only seven shops were listed: Xingda, Chengyu, Xingkang, Yuankang, Hengmao, etc. However, they all reduced their scale and did not release large amounts of funds, and there were few bad debt burdens. Although there were slight profits at the end of the year, it was only a matter of appearance. It is said that two more shops will close down this year. The money shop industry is being eliminated by the times, and it is feared that it will no longer have a place in the commercial world.

Rice Business: Wuhu's rice business is divided into purchasing and transportation, rice shops, rice hulling mills, and rice milling. In recent years, due to the dumping of foreign rice in South China, merchants from Guangdong and Chaozhou were forced to shut down, causing the rice market to plummet. Last year, if it were not for merchants from Yantai, Nanjing, Shanghai, and Wuhan, as well as the continuous purchase of military rice, there would have been hardly any rice market to speak of. In the past, the annual export of rice reached eight million shi (a unit of dry measure), but last year it was only about 1.3 to 1.4 million shi. At the end of the year, rice shops from Guangdong and Chaozhou, and Jiangguang rice merchants suffered huge losses due to not having done business for many years. However, rice mills and rice hulling mills all received rice for stockpiling. At that time, the cost was six yuan and several jiao per dan (another unit of dry measure). Later, due to the scarcity of supply, the market price gradually rose, and each dan had to be sold for ten silver dollars. All those who had not sold their rice made huge profits.

Yarn Industry: Wuhu's larger industries are still in their infancy. There is only one yarn factory, Yuzhong, which was founded by Li Boxing and others. It has been in operation for more than ten years and has never made a profit. It has been reorganized several times, but its business is still sluggish. The total accumulated losses over the years amount to more than one million yuan. As for the yarn shops that sell cotton yarn, there are more than a dozen, and their business is relatively stable. Their capital is also very strong, especially Shiyu and Tongchun, whose businesses are the largest. At the end of last year, all yarn shops had profits.

Cloth Industry: Wuhu's silk and cloth industry has suffered losses in recent years due to the plummeting prices of silk goods. In addition, due to the impact of the situation and tight credit, no one has not reduced its scale, and business has gradually declined. In the spring and summer of last year, business was mediocre. By the autumn, businesses competed with each other, offering special discounts and gifts, such as Gongxing, Dacheng, Renji, Qingda, Changxie, and Hongzhang. Transactions were slightly more developed, but expenses were heavy. After the closing, most businesses had mixed fortunes. Gongxing, Qingda, and Changdacheng, etc., still had several thousand taels of silver in profits due to their thicker capital.

Southern Goods: There are more than 100 southern goods businesses of all sizes registered with the trade association. Their business is still not bad, because the goods they sell are necessities for people's daily lives. In the past, Fushengtai from Fujian and Wang Yulong from Anhui were the leaders in the industry. Their annual turnover was about 300,000 yuan. In recent years, due to the market situation, people's purchasing power has weakened, and transactions have been greatly reduced. Wang Yulong has closed down, and Fushengtai's annual turnover is also less than 100,000 yuan. If one business is like this, the situation of other businesses can be imagined. From spring to winter last year, prices were stable, and there was generally no profit to be made. However, in November of winter, oil prices soared, and all those with large inventories made huge profits.

In addition, industries such as hardware, timber, pawnshops, medicine, general merchandise, soap, dyeing, silver shops, restaurants, and paper have all had less business than in previous years, and it can be said that there are no profits. It is said that many shops will close down this year. This state of decline has not been seen in decades. (8th)

Hubei Provincial Department of Finance Holds Provincial Tax Conference 121

The conference will last for three days, and more than twenty major cases will be resolved.

Reorganizing the tax system and abolishing excessive and miscellaneous taxes are the focus of discussion.

Hankou Correspondence: In order to reorganize the tax system of the province and thoroughly abolish excessive and miscellaneous taxes, the Department of Finance has convened a provincial tax conference. Shen Fan, Director of the Hankou Business Tax Bureau, Tao Zuguang, Director of the Wuchang Business Tax Bureau, Xiong Zengshou, Director of the Yichang Business Tax Bureau, Li Jie, Director of the Shashi Business Tax Bureau, Xu Naiji, Director of the Wuxue Business Tax Bureau, Xie Chengxuan, Director of the Yuekou Business Tax Bureau, Xu Linxiang, Director of the Guangshui Business Tax Bureau, Wang Xiubei, Director of the Laohekou Business Tax Bureau, Zhang Daquan, Director of the Yangloudong Business Tax Bureau, Zhou Boxiang, Director of the Tuanfeng Business Tax Bureau, Tong Binqiu, Director of the Wuyang Tax Collection Office, and Sha Fengwu, Director of the Wuyang Tobacco and Alcohol License Bureau, were all summoned to the province. The conference opened on the 6th and held its first meeting. Proposals from various parties were divided into administrative and tax groups for review. The review was completed on the 7th, and a second meeting was held on the 8th, focusing on the reorganization of taxes and the abolition of excessive and miscellaneous taxes. More than twenty cases were decided, roughly: (1) Dividing tax collection areas. The business tax of seventeen small counties in northwestern Hubei will be collected by the nearby Business Tax Bureau. (2) Regularly carrying out province-wide inspections of shop ledgers to prevent concealment. (3) Establishing waterway checkpoints to prevent evasion. (4) Urging the collection of new and old outstanding taxes, with tax reductions and exemptions for disaster areas. (5) Reorganizing the brewing industry and banning pawnshop agencies. (6) Thoroughly abolishing excessive and miscellaneous taxes to reduce the burden on the people. (7) Increasing the salaries of staff in various tax bureaus and strictly defining rewards and punishments to encourage and warn them. The closing ceremony was held that evening. (8th)

Jiading Bandit Leader Guo Amao Arrested 122

Guo Amao from Guojiacun, Naxiang, formerly robbed Cantonese people in the vicinity. He was sentenced to imprisonment by the county. During the Japanese occupation of the county, he escaped from prison. There were still seven years left in his sentence. After the county was restored, he was wanted by the High Court. He hid in other places and continued to break the law. On the one hand, he colluded with lake bandits, and on the other hand, he colluded with local gangsters. In the autumn of the 21st year, he gathered a group to rob two rifles from the Chaxi Self-Defense Force. The robbery cases in the southwest countryside last winter were also closely related to Guo. He recently sneaked back to his hometown and hid in the home of relatives in Pengjiacun nearby. This was discovered by the Chaxi Sentinel. They met with Zhang Tiange, the patrol chief of the Naxiang Public Security Substation, and went to arrest him at 1:00 a.m. on the 2nd. Guo heard the sound and tried to escape through the roof, but was arrested and taken to the Naxiang Substation. After interrogation by Patrol Officer Cao Hanqing, he confessed that Chen Kunlin from Fang Taixi Township was his accomplice. That night, Chen was also arrested.

Wuxi Implements Cocoon Market Control 123

This county is implementing cocoon market control. Last year, the cocoon merchants repeatedly requested that it be postponed for one year, which was approved. The spring cocoon season is approaching soon. The Construction Department believes that this county is the central area of sericulture in the province and should actively promote control to achieve the purpose of improvement. Guan Yida was specially sent to Wuxi to contact the cocoon merchants' association and decided to implement control this year. Five principles were drafted and submitted to the provincial capital for approval and implementation.

Department Commissioner Inspects Charitable Institutions 124

In order to understand the situation of charitable undertakings in various counties in Jiangsu Province and improve them, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs specially appointed Xiang Dating to inspect Wuxi. Yesterday, Commissioner Xiang, accompanied by Feng Baoyi, a staff member of the county government, and Qin Zhenhua of the Relief Home, first went to Chong'an Temple Hengshantang, as well as the Free Clinic, Infant Home, and Tongrentang, etc., to visit. Then he went to the Civilian Vocational Training Center outside the South Gate to visit the rope-making, box-making, and sewing workshops. Finally, he investigated Pujitang and visited the nursing home. The home takes care of one hundred elderly people over the age of 60, who gathered in a hall, standing respectfully to await Commissioner Xiang's personal condolences before dispersing. It is planned to continue investigating all public and private hospitals in the county today.

Robbery and Assault Case Occurs in the Southern Suburbs of Changzhou 125

The family of Wang Jinhai, a villager in Hehuatang near Liaoyipu in the southern suburbs of Wuyi, has some assets and is quite well-off. Unexpectedly, at about 1:00 a.m. on the 7th, more than ten armed bandits suddenly came, broke into the house, twisted the homeowner Wang Jinhai, and demanded silver dollars. Wang resisted at the time, causing him to be stabbed once by the bandits, and his right forehead was severely injured. During the struggle, one of the bandits was also cut. The bandits then searched at will and took away silver dollars, clothing, and other items.

Jiangyin Villager Killed While Performing Dragon Lantern Dance 126

In Huangdan, ten miles west of the city in the western countryside of the seventh district, the village was disturbed by the bandit Gao Xiaosheng the year before last, and the villagers were almost turned into bandits. After Gao was brought to justice, the area gradually became peaceful. The day before yesterday (the 5th) was the second day of the first lunar month of the old calendar. The villagers there started a large dragon lantern dance, going back and forth in the village, in high spirits. Later, due to the "dazhao" relationship (dragon lanterns are greeted with firecrackers, and must be carried back and forth, called "dazhao"), it led to a conflict between villagers. A villager, Kuang Yingen, was hit in the head by a long bench, causing serious injuries and death. Subsequently, the local merchant group arrested Xie Chunyuan, Xie Chunlin, Xu Fugeng, Geng Taili, and Zhou Henggui, the five people who were performing the lantern dance, and sent them to the county on the 7th. In the morning, Judge Jiang went to the countryside to examine the body. On the same day, a nameless male corpse was found in the third section of Houmei, with injuries, seemingly thrown into the river after being sexually assaulted. Judge Jiang did not return to the city until the afternoon of the 8th.

Commerce After the Year-End Closing 127

Cheng County's commerce was affected by the drought and famine last year, coupled with the decline of the rural economy. It can be said that all industries were depressed. The accounts after the year-end closing were only 50-60%. Fortunately, the money shop industry was still good. The most developed cloth factory industry, such as Huacheng, with a larger scale, still had a lot of inventory and poor sales, and its business was far from what it used to be. The other public welfare Rongxi factories only weave customized goods and have a small profit. The silk and cloth industry has declined sharply because the traffic between Xicheng and Zhencheng is convenient, and buyers tend to go to other ports. Many businesses have closed down, such as Wanyusen. The remaining yarn and rice industries are just stable.

Zhenjiang Department of Finance Issues Circular to Various Bureaus and Offices, Instructing on Fire Prevention 128

The Department of Finance recently issued instructions to the Danyang Puzhen Vegetable and Cattle Inspection Office of various business tax bureaus and collection offices, saying that the agencies under the department are responsible for collection and are very important. Fire prevention must be implemented. The points that should be noted are listed on the left: (1) The house you live in is best to be a detached house, and there must be an emergency exit. Those who live upstairs must pay special attention to the convenience of the staircase exit. If you live with the landlord or other tenants, you must be separated from each other and not live together in a mixed manner. (2) There must be a well or water stored in a tank. Do not pile up flammable materials, or use kerosene stoves and other things in the bedroom, so as to be prepared for emergencies. (3) The taxes collected, whether cash or banknotes, must be sent to the treasury for deposit and must not be kept privately. (4) Blank receipts received from the department, or those that have been used but not reported and verified, as well as various account books, etc., should be collected in one place every night and stored safely in a locked wicker box or other box, so that they can be easily moved in case of an emergency. (5) Every night or on holidays, responsible personnel must be assigned to stay in the agency and must not leave completely. All of the above points should be paid special attention to and strictly followed. In addition, if there are other fire prevention procedures, they should also be supplemented and handled as appropriate.

Letter

Letter from Songjiang Telephone Company 129

Dear Editor: I read a letter in your newspaper from the Songjiang Electric and Steam Company, which stated that the telephone poles were knocked down in as many as nine places due to snow. This is very surprising. Upon investigation, our company's lines only had poles leaning against the stone archway at Beicang Bridge, and the focal point was not there, but at the entrance of Chayuan Lane. The electric light company exaggerated the situation in order to avoid the use of sheathed wire at the intersection and shift the blame to our company. Therefore, we hereby declare, and hope you will check and correct it. Sincerely, Songjiang Telephone Company, September 9th.

Special Article

A Review of the World Economy in 1934 (4) by Ou Muchu 130

Stock prices rose across the board, except in countries that maintained the gold standard. Low interest rates especially proved the surplus of capital. This is evidence that a chronic economic panic is still continuing.

Moreover, the foundation of the panic is built on overproduction. We dare not say that the reason why the world economy in 1934 has escaped the panic is because overproduction still exists. Various "production restrictions" and "production reduction agreements" are clear evidence. However, "production restriction" is neither a reasonable economic law, nor does it have the danger of making things more confusing. In addition, the budget of various countries has a large deficit, and there must be an urgent method to overcome the economic crisis, so seizing and promoting new markets for surplus goods has become the only means for the great powers. Therefore, some countries used the opportunity to plunder the territory of other countries as colonies; for example, Japan forcibly seized my Northeast provinces. Some countries, due to geographical relations, have to use their economic power to conquer the world in order to expand the market, such as the United States' abandonment of the gold standard, the implementation of currency inflation, and the devaluation of exchange rates. Of course, the adoption of political and military power to expand its market has not forgotten the use of its economic power. We will not talk about the use of political and military plunder of the world market for the time being. Here we only talk about the general situation of the competition for the market by economic power. The fact that the great powers used their superior economic power to plunder the world market was most obvious in 1934. Now we will list a few important facts as follows:

(1) Currency Inflation The amount of banknotes in circulation is the best example of currency inflation. The table below lists the amount of banknotes in circulation in major countries in the world:

Although the increase between 1933 and 1934 is very small, it is because of the compensation for public debt. And the debts of various countries have now reached saturation. The deficit in the future can no longer be taken from public debt, and the scope of currency inflation will inevitably be further expanded, which is worthy of our attention.

Local News

Five Banks Organize Agricultural Loan Group, Established Yesterday 131

This year's investment amount is set at 3 million yuan

Hope other banks will participate in cooperation

Central News Agency reports that the Agricultural Cooperative Loan Group organized by the Bank of Communications, Jincheng Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Shanghai Commercial and Savings Bank, and Four Provinces Farmers Bank held an establishment meeting at the Bank of Communications on the Bund yesterday afternoon at 3:00 p.m. It was resolved to elect executive directors and approve several important cases, such as the amount of loans to be released. The details are as follows:

Start of Meeting 132

Those who attended the meeting yesterday included Li Zhongchu of the Bank of Communications, Wu Xiaoyuan of Jincheng Bank, Yang Yinpu of Zhejiang Industrial Bank (representing Shi Daochun), Zou Bingwen of Shanghai Commercial and Savings Bank, and Zhu Runsheng of Four Provinces Farmers Bank. The meeting started at 3:00 p.m.

Election of Executive Directors 133

The representatives of the five banks are all directors. Li Zhongchu and Zou Bingwen were elected as executive directors from among the five directors. The organization of the group completely adopts the form of the General Administration Office. In the future, offices will be established in Henan, Hebei, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shaanxi to directly manage investment matters in each province and obey the command of the group. The establishment of the offices will have to wait for some time, as all procedures are still under discussion.

Investment Amount 134

As for the banks' investment in rural areas, it has already started last year. However, the five banks acted individually. In the past year, Shaanxi Province was the only one limited, with an amount of about one million yuan. This time, the banks, in view of the importance of investing in rural areas, decided to adopt an overall plan to unify it. At yesterday's meeting, it was decided that the investment amount for this year will be limited to 3 million yuan.

Office Location 135

At yesterday's meeting, the group also decided to temporarily use the Bank of Communications as its office. In order to achieve the effect of gathering strength and wisdom, the group very much hopes that other banks will participate in this initiative. In the future, if other banks participate, each bank can appoint a representative to serve as a director, so as to jointly discuss the method of investing in rural areas. Currently, apart from the five banks, no other banks have formally expressed their participation, but it is expected that the number of participating banks will increase after a considerable period of time.

Discussion of Regulations 136

The group's regulations have now been drafted and were submitted for discussion at yesterday's meeting. However, the regulations are of great importance and should be considered with extra care. Therefore, at yesterday's meeting, although a long time was spent researching and revising them, it was still felt that there were some imperfections. It was resolved that the directors would further study them separately outside the meeting and then submit them to the next meeting for discussion.

Financial Advisory Committee Did Not Establish as Scheduled Yesterday 137

Due to Minister Kong Suffering from a Slight Cold

Central News Agency reports that after the Ministry of Finance hired Li Fuxun and other fourteen people as members of the Financial Advisory Committee, the inaugural meeting was originally scheduled to be held at the Central Bank yesterday afternoon at 4:00 p.m. However, due to Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi suffering from a slight cold and not yet fully recovered, it was not established as scheduled. Therefore, the establishment date of the committee will be decided and notified to the members after Minister Kong recovers, so that the inaugural meeting can be convened.

League of Nations Expert, Woermodo, Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 138

Scheduled to Return to Europe on the 13th

Mr. Woermodo, a League of Nations water conservancy expert, having previously visited various parts of North and Northwest China to inspect water conservancy projects such as the Yellow River and the Jingwei Canal, returned to Beijing a few days ago. Considering his term in China was complete, he immediately drafted a report on his observations and research results. After finishing this task, he bid farewell to the relevant authorities in Beijing and, accompanied by his secretary, Mr. Sattley, arrived in Shanghai at 7:15 AM yesterday on the night express train. He immediately visited Mr. Haas, the League of Nations Liaison for Technical Cooperation in China, to report everything. He has also decided to return to Europe on the Italian postal ship "Conte Verde" on the 13th of this month. According to Mr. Wu Xiufeng, a League of Nations secretary on leave returning to China, the proposals from various parties in our country to retain Mr. Woermodo for further work in China have now become a thing of the past. Mr. Woermodo believes that his mission to China was solely to assist in Chinese water conservancy. The results of his inspection showed that the Yellow River dredging project is the most important, but it requires an estimated 100 million yuan, which is beyond the current financial capacity. Therefore, Mr. Woermodo believes that there is currently no need for him to remain in China and, as his term in China has ended, he has decided to return to Europe first. It is reported that Mr. Woermodo is Italian and serves as a reporter for the League of Nations Committee on Communications and Public Works. He was hired to come to China at the beginning of November last year.

Huang Fu Entertains Japanese Press Corps 140

Hopes Japanese Will Treat China with Sincerity

The Japanese newspaper "Mainichi Shimbun" reported on the 9th that Mr. Huang Fu, Chairman of the Beiping Political Affairs Committee, who arrived in Shanghai on the 2nd, entertained the Japanese press corps stationed in Shanghai at his private residence on Qiqi Road in the French Concession on the 8th. The meeting lasted for 50 minutes, and the content was as follows: "My health has almost recovered, but my hand is still not comfortable and my blood pressure is also low, so I will stay in Shanghai for medical treatment until the end of this month. Next month, I will go to my hometown of Hangzhou for about a week, and then return to Shanghai, transfer to Nanjing, and return to Beiping. Chairman Jiang has gone to Nanchang. When I met with Jiang before, there was nothing special. There are many rumors outside about whether I will take office as Minister of the Interior, but I have not yet made a decision. If the situation changes, it is also possible to take office. When Chairman Jiang and Lieutenant General Suzuki and Yoshiya Company representatives held talks in Nanjing before, I also attended the meeting. This meeting can enable both China and Japan to understand each other with sincerity. Chairman Jiang has no personal grievances against Japan at all. Since the anti-communist movement began, he has long had the intention of cooperating with Japan. The cooperation between China and Japan is indeed the best policy to ensure peace in the East. China's past history is sufficient to prove this. However, since the Jinan Incident, the relationship between China and Japan has gradually deteriorated. This was not the original intention of the two peoples, and it was caused by sudden disasters. In the future, it is expected that the two peoples will restore a normal state. As for the specific preconditions between China and Japan, we must first start with sincerity. When the former South Da General went to Manchuria to take office, he said, 'We must first remove the sense of superiority of the Japanese in Manchuria, and then we can adjust the relationship between China and Japan.' The Japanese sense of superiority and China's anti-Japanese sentiment are mutually causal. If both are allowed to go unchecked, they will inevitably fall into an irretrievable situation. Therefore, please ask Japan to first remove the long-standing sense of superiority in China and transform it into an equal attitude, then China can naturally remove the resentment of anti-Japanese sentiment. This is the prerequisite for the rapprochement between China and Japan, and the people of both countries can consolidate cooperation with sincerity. The way to permanent peace in the East lies within this. Originally, human society is quite complex, and it is impossible to judge the whole by one part. We should open our eyes and take into account the overall situation. If there are occasional isolated phenomena, and we consider it to be a general problem, this kind of observation is extremely dangerous. If Japan is willing to abandon suspicion and treat China with sincerity, how can China abandon this good neighbor and not listen to cooperation? I hope that in the future, we will show each other our hearts and restore normal relations," he said.

Jiejian Company's Qitai Steamer Aground 148

Shallow Water in Tongzhou Makes Towing Ineffective

The Qitai steamer of Jiejian Company originally operated on the Sichuan River route. In recent days, due to the large reduction in river water in the Yichang-Yibin section, the steamer came to Shanghai from Yichang, fully loaded with grains and other items. Because the steamer's draft was shallower than the river steamers of other companies, it was safe and sound. On the 6th of this month, when the steamer reached the Tongzhou river surface, it encountered a high tide with turbulent water. The Qitai was also a fully loaded steamer, making it difficult to resist. The captain, in order to ensure the safety of navigation, immediately dropped anchor and stopped to avoid the brunt of the tide. When the anchor was dropped, the water scale in the river was measured to be more than eight feet. The captain planned to wait for the water to settle down a bit before sailing, but unexpectedly, the water suddenly receded, and the rate of decrease was even more unexpected. It suddenly receded to five feet, and the Qitai ran aground.

Patrol Ship Rescue Ineffective 149

The captain was unable to move away from the sandbar and sent out a distress signal, which was detected by the Jianghai Customs patrol ship. The patrol ship immediately sailed to the location where the Qitai was aground to assist in towing, but even with full power, it could not be moved at all. The water level was continuing to decrease. The Customs patrol ship saw that the situation was not good and immediately stopped towing and sailed away. If it had been a step slower, the patrol ship would also have been stranded. The captain had no choice but to wire the Shanghai company to request a steamer to come to the rescue.

Yian Goes to the Rescue 150

Upon receiving the report, the Jiejian Company immediately dispatched the Yian steamer to the Tongzhou sandbar yesterday morning to find a way to tow it. Yesterday afternoon, according to the company's news, the Yian steamer arrived at the location where the Qitai steamer was aground and attempted to tow it, but it also failed. The company plans to have the Yian tow it again during high tide. If it is still ineffective, a tugboat will be sent from Shanghai to unload the cargo, reduce its weight, and then tow it.

Statistics of Shanghai Goods Shipped to the United States in January This Year 151

Increased Sharply Compared to the Same Period Last Year

The U.S. Consulate General in Shanghai announced yesterday the statistics of Shanghai's exports to the United States in January of this year. The total value was US$1,853,451, which is a large increase compared to the average total value of the twelve months of last year. The total value of Shanghai's exports to the United States for the entire last year was US$12,153,764. Among the exports in January, inedible plant products (excluding fiber wood) ranked first, accounting for US$572,070. Next were animal and animal products, accounting for US$569,471. Next were textiles, accounting for US$559,673.

Reportedly, Pirates Are Active Again in Dapeng Bay

The "Great American Evening News" reports that the Tongzhou ship sailed to Yantai again after 10:00 AM today (the 9th). However, when the ship set sail, Simat still came to the dock to take care of the children, and all the children cheered to him, because Simat risked his life to protect the children during the piracy, so they were moved and expressed their gratitude to him.
